\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item JIT\+: Optimize universal selector usage by inlining only the relevant selectors (\href{https://github.com/tailwindlabs/tailwindcss/pull/4850}{\texttt{ \#4850}}))

This provides a very significant performance boost on pages with a huge number of DOM nodes, but there\textquotesingle{}s a chance it could be a breaking change in very rare edge cases we haven\textquotesingle{}t thought of. Please open an issue if anything related to shadows, rings, transforms, filters, or backdrop-\/filters seems to be behaving differently after upgrading.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_node__modules_2tailwindcss_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md32052}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md_node__modules_2tailwindcss_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md32052}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The {\ttfamily presets} feature had unexpected behavior where a preset config without its own {\ttfamily presets} key would not extend the default config. (\href{https://github.com/tailwindlabs/tailwindcss/pull/2662}{\texttt{ \#2662}})

If you were depending on this unexpected behavior, just add {\ttfamily presets\+: \mbox{[}\mbox{]}} to your own preset to exclude the default configuration.
